function enable_scheme(npc, ini)

  reset_npc_logic(npc)
  
  local st = xr_logic.assign_storage_and_bind(npc, ini, "companion")
  
  if st then
    if xr_companion.is_companion(npc:id()) then
    st.enabled = true  
    end  
  end
end

function companion_start_following(npc, actor)
  sak.make_enemy_free(npc)
  local st = db.storage[npc:id()]
  local st_c = db.storage[npc:id()].companion
  if st and st_c then
    xr_companion.companions[npc:id()] = "companion"
    st_c.enabled = true  
  end
end

–≤–æ—Ç —ç—Ç–æ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏—è –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∏ –∂–µ?
function is_companion(npc_id)
  if npc_id then
    if companions[npc_id] and companions[npc_id] == "companion" then
      return true
    end
  end
  return false
end

function reset_npc_logic(obj)
  if obj then
    local npc_id = obj:id()
    db.storage[npc_id].overrides = nil
    xr_logic.reset_generic_schemes_on_scheme_switch(obj, "nil", "nil")
    db.storage[npc_id].active_section = nil
    db.storage[npc_id].active_scheme = nil
  end
end

function evaluator_karavan:evaluate()
  return db.actor
    and xr_logic.is_active( self.object, self.st )
    and self.st.enabled == true
end

function save_var_companion(npc, var_name, var_value)
  if not npc or not var_name then return end
  local sobj = alife():object(npc)
  if sobj then
  local pk = get_netpk( sobj, 1 )
  ASSERT( ( pk and pk:isOk() ), "can't read netpacket of %s", sobj:name() )
  local data = pk:get()
  data.custom_data[var_name] = var_value
  pk:set( data )
  end
end

function load_var_companion(npc, var_name, def_value)
  if not npc or not var_name then return end
  local sobj = alife():object(npc)
  if sobj then
  local pk = get_netpk( sobj, 1 )
  ASSERT( ( pk and pk:isOk() ), "can't read netpacket of %s", sobj:name() )
  local data = pk:get()
    if data.custom_data[var_name] then
      return custom_data[var_name]
    else  
      return def_value or nil
    end
  end  
end

–≤—ã–∑–æ–≤ –≤—Ä–æ–¥–µ —Ç–∞–∫ 
local cur_level_name = load_var_companion(npc_id,"c_lvl","none")

save_var_companion(npc_id,"c_lvl",level.name())

function is_companion(npc_id)
  if npc_id then
    if companions[npc_id] and companions[npc_id] == "companion" then
      return true
    end
  end
  return false
end

local team_smtr_assigned = {}
function se_smart_terrain:enabled(obj)
  --// xr_companion
  local st = db.storage[obj.id]
  if st then
    st = db.storage[obj.id].companion
  end
  
  if st and rx_karavan.is_companion(obj.id) then
    local npc_level = alife():level_name(game_graph():vertex(obj.m_game_vertex_id):level_id())
    if npc_level == level.name() 
    -- or st.behavior == xr_companion.beh_wait_simple 
    -- or st.behavior == xr_companion.beh_wait_low_aggr 
    -- or st.behavior == xr_companion.beh_wait_ignore 
    -- or st.behavior == xr_companion.beh_hide_simple 
    -- or st.behavior == xr_companion.beh_hide_low_aggr 
    -- or st.behavior == xr_companion.beh_hide_ignore   
    then
      team_smtr_assigned[obj.id] = nil
      return false
    else
      if team_smtr_assigned[obj.id] == self.id then
        return true
      elseif team_smtr_assigned[obj.id] then
        return false
      else
        -- mylog("assigning ".. self:name() .. " to " .. obj:name() .. " on " .. npc_level)
        team_smtr_assigned[obj.id] = self.id
        return true
      end
    end
  end  
  --// xr_companion

function se_smart_terrain:suitable( obj )
  if rx_karavan.is_companion(obj.id) and team_smtr_assigned[obj.id] == self.id then
    return 100000
  end

-- –≤—ã–¥–∞—Ç—å –æ–±—ä–µ–∫—Ç—É –∑–∞–¥–∞–Ω–∏–µ.
function se_smart_terrain:task( obj )
  --// xr_companion
    if rx_karavan.is_companion(obj.id) then
      rx_karavan.update_level_names(obj.id)
      local dest = rx_karavan.get_offline_dest()
      return CALifeSmartTerrainTask(dest)
    end
  --// xr_companion

function se_smart_terrain:smart_terrain_accepts_obj( obj, obj_agreement )
    if rx_karavan.is_companion(obj.id) then
    log1(tostring(obj.id))
      if not self:check_preset( community, obj:rank(), self.gparams.preset_name ) then
        return false
      end
    else
      if obj_agreement ~= agreed_exclusive and not self:check_preset( community, obj:rank(), self.gparams.preset_name ) then
        return false
      end
    end

–∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è –∫–æ—Å–Ω—É–≤—à–∏–µ—Å—è smart_terrain.script
local team_smtr_assigned = {} -- –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏–º —ç—Ç—É —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫—É –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥
function se_smart_terrain:enabled(obj)
–¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏–º 
  if xr_companion and xr_companion.obj_id_in_team(obj.id) then
  -- –ï—Å–ª–∏ NPC –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç—Å—è –Ω–∞ –æ–¥–Ω–æ–º —É—Ä–æ–≤–Ω–µ —Å –ì–ì –∏–ª–∏ –¥–∞–Ω –ø—Ä–∏–∫–∞–∑ –æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∞—Ç—å—Å—è –Ω–∞ –º–µ—Å—Ç–µ, –≤—ã–∫–∏–¥—ã–≤–∞–µ–º –µ–≥–æ –∏–∑ —Å–º—Ç—Ä
  -- –∏–Ω–∞—á–µ –Ω–∞–∑–Ω–∞—á–∞–µ–º NP–° –∏–∑ –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥—ã –ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–π –ø–æ–ø–∞–≤—à–∏–π—Å—è —Å–º–∞—Ä—Ç-—Ç–µ—Ä—Ä–µ–π–Ω
    local npc_level = alife():level_name(game_graph():vertex(obj.m_game_vertex_id):level_id())
    if npc_level==level.name() then
      team_smtr_assigned[obj.id]=nil
      return false
    else
      if team_smtr_assigned[obj.id]==self.id then
        return true
      elseif team_smtr_assigned[obj.id] then
        return false
      else
        -- mylog("assigning ".. self:name() .. " to " .. obj:name() .. " on " .. npc_level)
        team_smtr_assigned[obj.id]=self.id
        return true
      end
    end
  end

function se_smart_terrain:suitable( obj )
–¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏–º
  if team_smtr_assigned[obj.id]==self.id then
  -- –ù–∞—à —á–µ–ª–æ–≤–µ–∫
    return 100000
  end

function se_smart_terrain:task( obj )
–¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏–º
  if xr_companion and xr_companion.obj_id_in_team(obj.id) then
    -- –ù–∞—à —á–µ–ª–æ–≤–µ–∫
    xr_companion.update_level_names()
    local dest=xr_companion.get_offline_dest()
--    mylog("Setting task " .. dest .. " for " .. obj:name())
    return CALifeSmartTerrainTask( dest )
  end

xr_sleeper.script
function evaluator_need_sleeper:evaluate ()
